multiple packages within the apiserver codebase:\\n\\n## Core Webhook Controller Architecture\\nThe foundation is the generic webhook controller (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`), which implements the `Webhook` type - an abstract admission plugin with infrastructure for both Admit and Validate operations. The `NewWebhook()` function creates instances accepting handler, configFile, sourceFactory, and dispatcherFactory parameters. The `Dispatch()` method serves as the entry point for webhook dispatch logic, orchestrating calls to the dispatcher with collected hooks from the source.\\n\\n## Webhook Dispatcher Implementations\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle the actual webhook invocation pattern:\\n\\n1. **Mutating Webhooks** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`): The `mutatingDispatcher` type implements the Dispatcher interface, iterating through webhooks and applying patches. The `callAttrMutatingHook()` method handles individual webhook calls, creates admission objects, verifies responses, and applies JSON patches to the object. Crucially, it manages webhook re-invocation context (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`), tracking which webhooks should be re-invoked if mutations occur.\\n\\n2. **Validating Webhooks** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`): The `validatingDispatcher` implements parallel webhook invocation using goroutines and WaitGroups. The `callHook()` method calls individual validation webhooks, and errors are collected and returned. This dispatcher caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions across parallel webhook calls.\\n\\n## Plugin Registration\\nThe mutating and validating plugins (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go` and `validating/plugin.go`) wrap the generic Webhook, exposing `Admit()` and `Validate()` methods that delegate to the underlying `Webhook.Dispatch()` call.\\n\\n## Admission Request/Response Handling\\nThe request package (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go`) manages AdmissionReview object creation and response verification. `CreateAdmissionObjects()` constructs v1 or v1beta1 AdmissionReview requests, while `VerifyAdmissionResponse()` validates responses and extracts audit annotations, patches, and warnings. `CreateV1AdmissionReview()` and `CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview()` handle version-specific object construction.\\n\\n## Webhook Accessors and Configuration\\nWebhook accessors (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`) provide abstraction over mutating and validating webhook configurations, enabling both v1 and v1beta1 access patterns. The initializer package (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/initializer/initializer.go`) handles plugin initialization with service resolvers and authentication info.\\n\\n## Admission Chain Integration\\nThe core chain handler (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go`) orchestrates the admission control chain, executing handlers in sequence for mutating and validating phases.
